<script src="https://bigwalldigital.com/wp-includes/js/jquery/jquery.min.js?ver=3.7.1" id="jquery-core-js"></script>
<script id="jquery-core-js-after">
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
            const header = document.querySelector('#masthead');
            if (!header) return;

            let lastScroll = 0;
            let isHidden = false;
            let ticking = false;

            // Ensure transition applies
            header.style.transition = 'transform 0.3s ease';
            header.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';

            function handleScroll() {
                const current = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;

                if (current > lastScroll && current > 80) {
                    // Scrolling DOWN → hide header
                    if (!isHidden) {
                        header.style.transform = 'translateY(-120%)';
                        isHidden = true;
                    }
                } else {
                    // Scrolling UP → show header
                    if (isHidden) {
                        header.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
                        isHidden = false;
                    }
                }

                lastScroll = current <= 0 ? 0 : current;
                ticking = false;
            }

            window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
                if (!ticking) {
                    window.requestAnimationFrame(handleScroll);
                    ticking = true;
                }
            });
        });
        
//# sourceURL=jquery-core-js-after
</script>

  transform: translate3d(0,0,0);
  animation-timing-function: ease-in-out;
  animation-iteration-count: infinite;
}

   PURE VERTICAL FLOAT
================================ */

  animation: float-vertical 5.6s infinite;
}

/* ===============================
   SUBTLE LEFT DRIFT
================================ */
.zerogravity2 {
  animation: float-left 4.8s infinite;
}

/* ===============================
   SUBTLE RIGHT DRIFT
================================ */
.zerogravity3 {
  animation: float-right 6.2s infinite;
}

/* ===============================
   LONGER ORBIT-LIKE DRIFT
================================ */
.zerogravity4 {
  animation: float-orbit 7.4s infinite;
}

/* ===============================
   KEYFRAMES
================================ */

/* Clean up & down */
@keyframes float-vertical {
  0%, 100% { transform: translateY(0); }
  50% { transform: translateY(-14px); }
}

/* Gentle left sway */
@keyframes float-left {
  0%, 100% { transform: translate(0, 0); }
  50% { transform: translate(-8px, -16px); }
}

/* Gentle right sway */
@keyframes float-right {
  0%, 100% { transform: translate(0, 0); }
  50% { transform: translate(8px, -12px); }
}

  0%   { transform: translate(0, 0); }
  25%  { transform: translate(6px, -8px); }
  50%  { transform: translate(0, -16px); }
  75%  { transform: translate(-6px, -8px); }
  100% { transform: translate(0, 0); }
}

<h2 id="gspb_heading-id-gsbp-e63739f" class="gspb_heading gspb_heading-id-gsbp-e63739f "><strong><strong><strong><strong><strong><strong><strong><strong><strong><strong><strong><strong>Why Big Wall?</strong></strong></strong></strong></strong></strong></strong></strong></strong></strong></strong></strong></h2>



<div id="whybigwall"></div><div id="gspb_text-id-gsbp-f11a794" class="gspb_text gspb_text-id-gsbp-f11a794 whybigwall">We could tell you why to choose us… but you’ve already seen the results. So instead, here’s why we’re called Big Wall Digital.<br><br>Big wall climbing is our passion — and the perfect metaphor for business and digital marketing. Tackling a big wall isn’t about quick wins; it’s about preparation, teamwork, strategy, and steady progress. You plan carefully, set anchors, and climb one pitch at a time. That’s exactly how we approach your digital growth: secure foundations, the right tools, and consistent execution that compounds over time.<br><br>Like climbers on a wall, we’re in it with you, focused, disciplined, and committed to helping you reach the summit.</div>

{"prefetch":[{"source":"document","where":{"and":[{"href_matches":"/*"},{"not":{"href_matches":["/wp-*.php","/wp-admin/*","/wp-content/uploads/*","/wp-content/*","/wp-content/plugins/*","/wp-content/themes/generatepress_child/*","/wp-content/themes/generatepress/*","/*\\?(.+)"]}},{"not":{"selector_matches":"a[rel~=\"nofollow\"]"}},{"not":{"selector_matches":".no-prefetch, .no-prefetch a"}}]},"eagerness":"conservative"}]}

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
    const swiperEl = document.querySelector(".gspb_slider-id-gsbp-d65f4f3 .swiper");
    if (!swiperEl || !swiperEl.swiper) return;

    const swiper = swiperEl.swiper;

    // Disable Swiper's built-in mousewheel
    if (swiper.mousewheel && typeof swiper.mousewheel.disable === "function") {
        swiper.mousewheel.disable();
    }

    let isScrolling = false;     // throttle flag
    const delay = 320;           // adjust speed (higher = slower + smoother)

    swiperEl.addEventListener("wheel", (e) => {
        const deltaY = e.deltaY;
        if (deltaY === 0) return;

        const atStart = swiper.isBeginning;
        const atEnd = swiper.isEnd;

        // THROTTLE: slow down scroll
        if (isScrolling) {
            e.preventDefault();
            return;
        }

        // --- SCROLL DOWN ---
        if (deltaY > 0) {
            if (!atEnd) {
                e.preventDefault();
                isScrolling = true;
                swiper.slideNext();
                setTimeout(() => isScrolling = false, delay);
                return;
            }
            return; // natural scroll after last slide
        }

        // --- SCROLL UP ---
        if (deltaY < 0) {
            if (!atStart) {
                e.preventDefault();
                isScrolling = true;
                swiper.slidePrev();
                setTimeout(() => isScrolling = false, delay);
                return;
            }
            return; // natural scroll before slide 1
        }

    }, { passive: false });

});
</script>
<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
  const section = document.querySelector("#gspb_row-id-gsbp-b66e769");
  if (!section) return;

  const maxFade = 1; // 1 = can go fully invisible, lower for partial fade

  function fadeBackground() {
    const rect = section.getBoundingClientRect();
    const sectionHeight = rect.height || 1;

    // Start fading after a *very slight scroll* (20px)
    const startOffset = 50;

    // Distance over which the fade happens (30% of section height)
    const fadeDistance = sectionHeight * 0.9;

    // How far we've scrolled past the start point
    const distance = Math.max(0, -rect.top + startOffset);

    // 0 → 1 over fadeDistance
    const progress = Math.min(distance / fadeDistance, 1);

    const opacity = 1 - progress * maxFade;
    section.style.opacity = opacity;
  }

  fadeBackground();
  window.addEventListener("scroll", fadeBackground);
  window.addEventListener("resize", fadeBackground);
});
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
	var textBlock = document.querySelector(".whybigwall");


    if (!textBlock) return;

    // Create button (only for mobile)
    var btn = document.createElement("div");
    btn.id = "mobile-readmore-btn";
    btn.innerText = "Read more";

    // Insert button after the text block
    textBlock.insertAdjacentElement("afterend", btn);

    btn.addEventListener("click", function () {
        textBlock.classList.toggle("expanded");
        btn.innerText = textBlock.classList.contains("expanded")
            ? "Read less"
            : "Read more";
    });
});
</script>

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {

  const overlay = document.querySelector('.modal-overlay');

  function closeModal() {
    document.body.classList.remove('modal-open');
    document.querySelectorAll('.modal.is-active')
      .forEach(m => m.classList.remove('is-active'));
  }

  document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#modal-"]').forEach(link => {
    link.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
      const modalClass = this.getAttribute('href').substring(1);
      const modal = document.querySelector('.modal.' + modalClass);

      if (!modal) return;

      e.preventDefault();
      closeModal();

      if (!modal.querySelector('.modal-close')) {
        modal.insertAdjacentHTML(
          'afterbegin',
          '<button class="modal-close" aria-label="Close modal">&times;</button>'
        );
        modal.querySelector('.modal-close')
          .addEventListener('click', closeModal);
      }

      document.body.classList.add('modal-open');
      modal.classList.add('is-active');
    });
  });

  overlay.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
  document.addEventListener('keydown', e => e.key === 'Escape' && closeModal());

});
</script>
